<triple> Baku_Turkish_Martyrs_Memorial | material | "Red granite and white marble"  </triple> <triple>  Baku_Turkish_Martyrs_Memorial | dedicatedTo | "Ottoman Army soldiers killed in the Battle of Baku"  </triple> <triple>  Baku_Turkish_Martyrs_Memorial | location | Azerbaijan  </triple> <triple>  Baku_Turkish_Martyrs_Memorial | nativeName | "Türk Şehitleri Anıtı"  </triple> <triple>  Azerbaijan | leaderName | Artur_Rasizade  </triple> <triple>  Baku_Turkish_Martyrs_Memorial | designer | "Hüseyin Bütüner and Hilmi Güner" </triple>	The Baku Turkish Martyrs' Memorial (designed by Huseyin Butuner and Hilmi Guner) is located in Baku, Azerbaijan.
